 yahaan ek vishesh dhanshodhan nirodhak adaalat main dhanshodhan nirodhak adhinium kii vibhinn dhaaraon ke tahat baari-bharkam anubandhon ke saath 57 prishthon kaa aarope patr yaa abhiyojan paksh kii shikaayat daayar kii
 The Enforcement Directorate had registered a criminal case under the PMLA in this deal last year and has so far confiscated assets worth Rs 9,600 crore

" '' white house main satta parivartan ke dauraan trump dwaara sheersh stareey prashasan ke liye chuni gayi punjab se bhartiya pravaasiyon kii 44 varshiya beti heli pehali mahila hai

" asked me to do
 '' Haley, who holds a second term as governor, has worked on trade and labor issues but has little experience in foreign policy

 Trump met Haley at the Trump Tower in New York last Thursday
 vah trump prashasan main shaamil kii jane vaali pehali mahila or alpsankhyak hongi, jo sanyukt raashtra main america kii agali rajdoot ke rup main samantha power kaa sthaan lengi
 Haley was vocal about Trump during the primary election and supported Senator Marco Rubio in the Republican primary
 haalanki, aam chunaavon ke pehle unhone apana rukh badalte hue kaha ki vah trump ko vot dengi
 Namrata 'nikki' Randhawa is South Carolina's first minority and female governor
 ruudhivaadee maane jane vaale is praant main nasleey sangharsh kaa lanbaa itihaas rahaa he
 Nikki Haley was a member of the province's House of Representatives from Lexinton County before becoming Governor of South Carolina from 2005 to 2011
 governor ke taur par heli ne apana loha manvaaya he tathaa berogari kii dar 15 saal main sabase nichle str par laa diya
 Under his leadership, over 82,000 jobs were created in each of the province's 46 counties
 tippaniyan She was involved in her family business before venturing into politics
 unke pati maaikel heli sena main captain hai jo afghanistan ke helmand praant main bhi seva de chuke hai
 They have two children, Reena (18) and Nalin (15)
 (hedline ke alaava, is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he, yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) trump ne kaha, ''garvanar heli ne apane praant or hamaare desh kii behatari ke liye mahatvapurn nitiyon ko aage badhane kii khatir logon ko unki prishthbhumi yaa party se judaav se itar saath laane kaa trek record sthapit kiya he
 44-year-old daughter Haley is the first woman of Indian migrants from Punjab elected by Trump to top-level administration during the transition to power at the White House
 navnirvaachit raashtrapati ne kaha, ''unhone khud ko samjhaute karaane main maahir hona sabit kiya he tathaa ham bahut saare samjhaute karaane ko lekar ashavan hai
 She will prove to be a great leader, representing us globally
 '' cabinet ke pad ke liye seenet kii manjuuri kii aavashyaktaa hogi
 After approval, she will be the first Indian American to achieve the status of a cabinet officer in any administration
 is pramukh pad ke liye namit hone ke baad heli ne kaha, ''hamaare desh ke saamne gharelu or antarrashtriya str par badi chunautiyaan khadi hai or main khud ko sammanit mahasoos karti hum ki navnirvaachit raashtrapati ne mujhase apni team main shaamil hone or desh kii seva karne ke liye kaha
 '' governor ke taur par doosraa kaarykaal sambhaal raheen heli kaarobaar or shram mudde par kaam kar chuki hai lekin unhen videsh niti kaa thodaa hi anubhav he
 His approach to various US military and national security issues has been within the purview of the Republican Party's thinking
 trump kii pichley guuruuvaar ko neuyork ke trump tower main heli se mulaakaat hui thi
 She will be the first woman and minority to be inducted into the Trump administration, replacing Samantha Power as America's next ambassador to the United Nations
 heli primary chunaav ke dauraan trump ko lekar mukhar thim or unhone republican primary main sinetter marco rubio kaa samarthan kiya tha
 However, before the general elections, she changed her stand and said that she would vote for Trump
